airplane_01,90,63,0	script	觸發#pc	-1,3,3,{
	end;

OnTouch:
	if ((prt_curse == 36 || prt_curse == 45 || prt_curse == 56 || prt_curse == 61) && (aru_monas < 1)) {
		hideoffnpc "情報員#pc1";
		mes "[????]";
		mes "你是"+strcharinfo(0)+"嗎?";
		mes "我正在等你呢，";
		mes "在^6B8E23普隆德拉教堂^000000 的 ^6B8E23'班波'^000000";
		mes "正在等你呢，";
		mes "請盡快去教堂一趟";
		set aru_monas,1;
		setquest 17000;
		close2;
		hideonnpc "情報員#pc1";
	}
	end;
}

cmd_in02,174,89,7	script	平凡的男人#pc1	97,{
	if (aru_monas < 2) {
		mes "[拉樂希司]";
		mes "喔，該死! 又輸了啦!";
		mes "這遊戲分明就是在耍老千啊";
		mes "無論玩多少次都是輸!";
		mes "不過這遊戲還挺讓人上癮的啊，呵呵";
		close;
	}
	else if (aru_monas == 2) {
		mes "[拉樂希司]";
		mes "哎呦呦...";
		mes "我到底輸了多少啊...";
		mes "嗚嗚嗚...";
		next;
		select("請..請問...");
		mes "[拉樂希司]";
		mes "哦 嗯...?";
		mes "有什麼地方可以幫助你的嗎?";
		next;
		select ("我是受^6B8E23班波祭司^000000之託而來的");
		mes "[拉樂希司]";
		mes "是這樣啊，我向您道歉啊";
		mes "如果得我的尖叫聲有嚇到你的話..";
		mes "我只是在這裡消磨時間啊，呵呵";
		mes "不過我現在已經認清賭博是個無底深淵啊!";
		next;
		mes "[拉樂希司]";
		mes "嗯.. 我們到那邊去談談吧";
		mes "小心隔牆有耳!";
		close2;
		set aru_monas,3;
		warp "cmd_in02",110,53;
		end;
	}
	else {
		mes "[拉樂希司]";
		mes "什麼!?  怎麼可能我又輸了!";
		mes "這遊戲機到底是該怎麼玩...";
		close;
	}
}

cmd_in02,111,52,3	script	平凡的男人#pc2	97,{

	}

		mes "據我調查的結果，";

		next;
		mes "[拉樂希司]";
		mes "然後他見了那個女人後，";
		mes "有其他人陸續進到他房間，然後帶著";
		mes "一個大袋子出了房門";
		next;
		mes "[拉樂希司]";
		mes "她們的背袋大得離譜，很奇怪吧?";
		mes "應該是有某組織的人預謀綁架了他";
		mes "而且把他帶到西邊的地區去了...";
		next;
		select("為什麼是西邊?");
		mes "[拉樂希司]";
		mes "這當然只是個猜測啦，";
		mes "不過我認為綁走他的人應該是";
		mes "來自^2F4F2F阿盧納貝茲^000000的人";
		mes "因為我不能進入阿盧納貝茲教國";
		mes "所以就無法取得更多消息了";
		set aru_monas,4;
		changequest 17001,17002;
		close;
	}
	else {
		mes "[拉樂希司]";
		mes "賭博輸了太多錢，";
		mes "這麼多負債怎麼還得起啊!";
		close;
	}
}

ra_in01,308,59,1	script	服務生#pc	930,{
	if (aru_monas < 7) {
		mes "[服務生]";
		mes "Welcome to";
		mes "Rachel's Palate, one";
		mes "of Rachel's finest and";
		mes "most exquisite restraunts.";
		if (aru_monas < 6) {
			close;
		}
		if (aru_monas == 6) {
			next;
			mes "[服務生]";
			mes "你是來用餐嗎?";
			mes "還是有其它事情?";
			next;
			if (select("我要用餐:我要辦事") == 1) {
				mes "[服務生]";
				mes "好的，沒問題?";
				mes "你是一個人來嗎?";
				next;
				select("是的");
				mes "[服務生]";
				mes "請往這邊走";
				close2;
				set aru_monas,7;
				switch(rand(1,4)) {
					case 1: warp "ra_in01",303,43; end;
					case 2: warp "ra_in01",304,43; end;
					case 3: warp "ra_in01",304,39; end;
					case 4: warp "ra_in01",303,39; end;
				}
			}
			mes "[服務生]";
			mes "嗯，不管要辦什麼事，";
			mes "希望你在拉赫玩得愉快";
			close;
		}
	}
	mes "[服務生]";
	mes "餐廳裡的每道菜都是拉赫..";
	mes "喔不! 是阿盧納貝茲裡最上等的喔!!";
	close;
}

	end;

z_agit,1,1,0	script	#zdan_broad	111,{
OnInit:
	disablenpc "#zdan_broad";
	stopnpctimer;
	end;

OnEnable:
	enablenpc "#zdan_broad";
	initnpctimer;
	hideonnpc "陸易";
	hideonnpc "瑪莎";
	hideonnpc "凱蒂";
	end;

OnDisable:
	disablenpc "#zdan_broad";
	stopnpctimer;
	end;

OnTimer3000:
	killmonster "z_agit","#ZGuard::OnMyMobDead";
	mapannounce "z_agit","凱蒂: Err? I heard something, meow! We must be under attack, meow!",bc_map,"0xFFFF00";
	end;

OnTimer5000:
	mapannounce "z_agit","陸易: Hey, 瑪莎! Are you the one who just got in?",bc_map,"0xFFFF00";
	end;

OnTimer7000:
	mapannounce "z_agit","瑪莎: 陸易, are you blind? I've been next to you this whole time! We'd better hide first.",bc_map,"0xFFFF00";
	end;

OnTimer9000:
	mapannounce "z_agit","陸易: We have an intruder! Hey, 凱蒂, what happened? Did you leave the entrance open?",bc_map,"0xFFFF00";
	end;

OnTimer11000:
	mapannounce "z_agit","凱蒂: No, impossible, meow~! I have a photographic memory!",bc_map,"0xFFFF00";
	end;

OnTimer13000:
	mapannounce "z_agit","瑪莎: Shut up, both of you! I don't know who you are, but you must have a lot of guts to mess with the Z集團!",bc_map,"0xFFFF00";
	end;

OnTimer15000:
	mapannounce "z_agit","陸易: 凱蒂, summon the soldiers! This is an emergency! Stop the intruder!",bc_map,"0xFFFF00";
	end;

OnTimer18000:
	mapannounce "z_agit","凱蒂: I haven't seen how strong they are, but... Meowkay. Guys, go out and fight!",bc_map,"0xFFFF00";
	end;

OnTimer21000:
	donpcevent "#ZGuard::OnEnable";
	end;

OnTimer300000:
	killmonster "z_agit","#ZGuard::OnMyMobDead";
	donpcevent "#zdan_broad::OnDisable";
	set $@monster_zgang,0;
	set $@door2,0;
	end;

OnTimer350000:
	mapwarp "z_agit","moc_fild17",209,235;
	hideonnpc "陸易";
	hideonnpc "瑪莎";
	hideonnpc "凱蒂";
	set $@monster_zgang,0;
	set $@door2,0;
	end;
}

-	script	#ZGuard	-1,{
OnInit:
	disablenpc "#ZGuard";
	end;

OnEnable:
	enablenpc "#ZGuard";
	initnpctimer;
	monster "z_agit",97,78,"凱蒂's Guard",1479,1,"#ZGuard::OnMyMobDead";
	monster "z_agit",98,79,"凱蒂's Guard",1479,1,"#ZGuard::OnMyMobDead";
	monster "z_agit",96,81,"凱蒂's Guard",1523,1,"#ZGuard::OnMyMobDead";
	end;

OnDisable:
	killmonster "z_agit","#ZGuard::OnMyMobDead";
	stopnpctimer;
	end;

OnReset:
	killmonster "z_agit","#ZGuard::OnMyMobDead";
	set $@monster_zgang,0;
	end;

OnMyMobDead:
	if (mobcount("z_agit","#ZGuard::OnMyMobDead") < 1) {
		mes "[" + strcharinfo(0) + "]";
		mes "You cowardly Z集團!";
		mes "Come out and surrender!";
		mes "I've defeated your monster";
		mes "soldiers already!";
		next;
		mes "[瑪莎]";
		mes "What should we do?";
		next;
		mes "[凱蒂]";
		mes "This is our greatest";
		mes "crisis ever! I don't";
		mes "know what to do, meow!";
		next;
		mes "[陸易]";
		mes "The Z集團's not going";
		mes "to surrender yet! Come";
		mes "forth, my loyal servants";
		mes "of the darkness!";
		next;
		mes "[凱蒂]";
		mes "No-no-no-meow!";
		mes "Not that button!";
		next;
		mes "[陸易]";
		mes "Huh? Why...?";
		next;
		set zdan_edq,17;
		donpcevent "#ZGuard::OnDisable";
		hideoffnpc "陸易";
		hideoffnpc "瑪莎";
		hideoffnpc "凱蒂";
		close;
	}
	end;

OnTimer300000:
	mapwarp "z_agit","moc_fild17",209,235;
	donpcevent "#zdan_broad::OnDisable";
	killmonster "z_agit","#ZGuard::OnMyMobDead";
	set $@monster_zgang,0;
	set $@door2,0;
	donpcevent "#ZGuard::OnDisable";
	stopnpctimer;
	end;
}

		close2;
		warp "moc_fild17",209,235;
		end;

	end;

morocc,143,63,3	script	邋遢的男子#nd	929,{
	if (treasure_nd == 0) {
		mes "[邋遢的男子]";
		mes "喂... 這位年輕人，";
		mes "幫幫我吧";
		next;
		mes "[邋遢的男子]";
		mes "沒錯，我說的就是你，";
		mes "你就當做救濟一個可憐的人，";
		mes "請答應我一個請求吧";
		next;
		switch(select("詢問是什麼事情:裝作沒聽見")) {
		case 1:
			mes "[" + strcharinfo(0) + "]";
			mes "好，請問是什麼事情呢?";
			next;
			mes "[邋遢的男子]";
			mes "唉喲~ 太感謝了，";
			mes "你真是現今社會罕見的";
			mes "好年輕人啊，";
			mes "之前有一些路過的年輕人，";
			mes "都裝作沒聽見就走過去了";
			next;
			mes "[邋遢的男子]";
			mes "好吧，我先自我介紹，";
			mes "嗯，嗯";
			next;
			mes "[邋遢的男子]";
			mes "別看我一副邋遢的樣子，";
			mes "其實我本來是尋找夢羅克";
			mes "寶藏的考古學家，";
			mes "出生地是普隆德拉";
			next;
			switch(select("所以呢?")) {
			case 1:
				mes "[邋遢的男子]";
				mes "其實我對寶藏方面";
				mes "充滿著信心，至少";
				mes "我一直認為對古書";
				mes "方面的專業，絕對";
				mes "超越任何人";
				next;
				mes "[邋遢的男子]";
				mes "我把全部積蓄花在研究上，";
				mes "到夢羅克去尋找寶藏，";
				mes "卻始終沒有任何發現，";
				mes "於是其他研究員陸續離開，";
				mes "我變成了窮光蛋";
				next;
				mes "[邋遢的男子]";
				mes "我... 現在，";
				mes "連回故鄉的車費都沒有，";
				mes "不僅白忙一場，結局又悲慘啊";
				emotion e_sob;
				next;
				mes "[邋遢的男子]";
				mes "所以我想跟你說，";
				mes "你能否捐點盤纏給我這";
				mes "可憐的學者，好讓我回到";
				mes "普隆德拉呢...?";
				next;
				switch(select("你走路回去吧:給一點是可以啦")) {
				case 1:
					mes "[邋遢的男子]";
					mes "哎~~";
					mes "是我看錯人了，";
					mes "好吧，那就請你離開吧";
					next;
					mes "[邋遢的男子]";
					mes "我本想有好康的事對你說，";
					mes "不過你我好像無緣哩";
					set treasure_nd,1;
					close;
				case 2:
					mes "[邋遢的男子]";
					mes "是嗎是嗎，非常感謝你，";
					mes "好心會有好報的...";
					next;
					if (Zeny < 1200) {
						mes "[邋遢的男子]";
						mes "不... 不過...";
						next;
						mes "[邋遢的男子]";
						mes "你自己好像也沒錢哩，";
						mes "是在哪兒遺失了嗎?";
						next;
						mes "[邋遢的男子]";
						mes "嗯哼...";
						mes "你只要有1200金幣，";
						mes "就能拿到重要的情報";
						set treasure_nd,1;
						close;
					}
					else {
						set zeny,zeny-1200;
						mes "[邋遢的男子]";
						mes "很好很好，用1200金幣";
						mes "就能換取物超所值的寶藏";
						mes "情報，算是撿到便宜了，";
						mes "你付的回故鄉旅費，";
						mes "非常感謝你...";
						next;
						mes "[邋遢的男子]";
						mes "普隆德拉，我回故鄉的旅費，";
						mes "已經足夠了，那麼";
						mes "告訴你一個情報當作回報吧";
						next;
						mes "[邋遢的男子]";
						mes "我所尋找的寶藏!";
						mes "聽說知道內幕的人，";
						mes "就住在夢羅克";
						mes "村落的北方";
						next;
						mes "[邋遢的男子]";
						mes "如果已被挖走就";
						mes "沒辦法了，但可以再問問看，";
						mes "或許還能挖得到";
						mes "其它情報";
						set treasure_nd,2;
						close;
					}
				}
			}
		case 2:
			mes "[邋遢的男子]";
			mes "喂~喂~";
			next;
			mes "[邋遢的男子]";
			mes "你是冒險家嗎...?";
			mes "我本想給你寶貴的情報，";
			mes "根本連聽都不想聽...";
			next;
			mes "[邋遢的男子]";
			mes "喂...喂...叫你呢...";
			close;
		}
	}
	else if (treasure_nd == 1) {
		mes "[邋遢的男子]";
